<main  class="content" id="site-main">
		<section  id="scope-tailwindcss">
						<div  class="content-container tw-space-y-16 !tw-pb-0">
								<div class="tw-flex tw-flex-col tw-items-start tw-gap-4">
					<h1 class="font-heading-3">
						Where female founders are gaining ground in venture capital					</h1>
											<p class="font-subtitle-1 tw-text-ui-400">
							The venture capital gender gap is no secret. Here’s a look top female founders VC funds, and advice from women in the startup world. 						</p>
									</div>
								<div class="tw-flex tw-flex-col tw-gap-6 md:tw-flex-row md:tw-justify-between">
					<div class="tw-flex tw-flex-col tw-gap-1">
						<em class="tw-not-italic font-subtitle-2">Written by Embroker Team</em>
						<em class="tw-not-italic font-label-2 tw-text-ui-400">Published April 24, 2025</em>
					</div>
				</div>
							</div>
		</section>
			<section >
		<div  class="content-container tw-max-w-[52rem] article-view">
			<div class="siege-interactive-post">
    <p>There’s this idea that Silicon Valley and, similarly, other tech hubs are these modern
        utopias
        where anyone can change the world with an idea — that is, if you’re a man. For women, it’s
        an
        uphill battle. Female founders continue to face endemic barriers in accessing capital to
        start
        and grow their businesses.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>The data is startling. Even with recent progress, companies founded solely by women garnered
        only
        <a href="https://pitchbook.com/news/articles/the-vc-female-founders-dashboard"
            target="_blank" rel="noopener">2.3 percent</a> of the total capital invested in
        venture-backed startups in
        the US. Not to mention, female partners are still a minority — 9 percent to be exact — with
        most
        dollars going into male-founded or mixed-gender startups.
    </p>

<!-- BLOCK block-cta-section/callout-version-04.twig START -->
<aside id="scope-tailwindcss" class="paper-flat callout callout-v4 tw-bg-green-300 article-view tw-space-y-4 tw-my-12 tw-p-8 !tw-text-ui-500 tw-w-full">
	<div class="tw-flex tw-flex-col md:tw-flex-row tw-items-center tw-gap-6">
				<div class="tw-shrink-0 md:tw-w-1/3">
						<img
			 src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAKAAAACxAQAAAABrPou+AAAAAnRSTlMAAHaTzTgAAAAaSURBVEjH7cExAQAAAMKg9U9tCy+gAAAA4GQOhQABjDooCwAAAABJRU5ErkJggg=="
				alt=""
			 class="!tw-m-0 md:tw-size-full lazyload"
			 data-src="https://website.embroker.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/frame_1321318687-1-1-min.png?strip=all&lossy=1&ssl=1" decoding="async" data-eio-rwidth="160" data-eio-rheight="177" /><noscript><img
				src="https://website.embroker.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/frame_1321318687-1-1-min.png?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1"
				alt=""
				class="!tw-m-0 md:tw-size-full"
			 data-eio="l" /></noscript>
		</div>
				<div class="tw-flex-grow">
							<em class="tw-block font-heading-4 tw-font-semibold tw-not-italic !tw-mb-4">Tailor a comprehensive insurance package.</em>
						<div>
				<p>Save time with Embroker&#8217;s single-destination solution.</p>

			</div>

    <p>Numerous reasons can be attributed to why the funding gap for women continues to be extremely
        wide. Among them is the fact that venture capital partnerships have historically been built
        by
        men and, with that, the trend of male-dominated funds has reigned supreme. But we’re not
        here to
        discuss what’s wrong with the VC <a href="https://www.embroker.com/blog/tech-gender-gap-study/"
            target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">gender gap</a>, how women must prove they
        deserve
        to be in an industry that’s male-dominated, or the frustrations that come with being the
        only
        woman in the room. Instead, we’re looking at where female founders are actually gaining
        ground.
    </p>
    <p>This guide takes a look at gender data to analyze the state of female startups, which
        metropolitan areas are leading the way for female-funded startups, and tips for women to
        navigate an industry that largely feels like a "brotopia.&nbsp;"</p>
    <h2>Leading metro areas for female-founded startups based on funding</h2>
    <p>Large metropolitan areas are naturally home to some of the most successful startups in the
        world.
        Big cities serve as <a href="https://www.embroker.com/blog/accelerators-vs-incubators/"
            target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">incubators</a> for creative ideas, wide
        customer
        bases, and, of course, close proximity to venture capitalists with deep pocketbooks. So, it
        goes
        without saying that these areas are favorable for startups regardless of their founder’s
        gender.&nbsp;</p>
    <p style="text-align: left;">That said, the gender gap is still significant across all 50 states
        and
        their major cities. Using <a
            href="https://pitchbook.com/news/articles/the-vc-female-founders-dashboard"
            target="_blank" rel="noopener">Pitchbook data</a>, we looked at which metropolitan
        statistical areas offer
        up the most capital invested and the greatest number of deals in solely female-founded
        startups.
        Here’s a look at the top 25 metropolitan areas for female founders based on the current U.S.
        data.&nbsp;</p>
    <div>

    <h3>&nbsp;</h3>
    <h3>Deal stage of top metropolitan areas</h3>
    <p>Of course, not all deals are created equal. Raising seed funding is significantly easier than
        <a href="https://www.embroker.com/blog/series-a-funding-strategy/">raising Series A</a> and beyond. In
        fact, it’s thought that the “seed surge” — this easy access to early-stage funding — gives a
        lot
        of founders a false sense of confidence when going into their Series A and beyond.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>Using the chart below, you can dive deeper into what the different deal stages look like for
        female-founded startups across each of the metropolitan areas highlighted in the map. The
        data
        is specifically divided into the following deal stages: angel/seed funding, early-stage VC
        (Series A) and later-stage VC (Series B and C).&nbsp;</p>
    <div>

    <h2>How’s the data trending?</h2>
    <p>We all know the VC gender gap is wide, but it’s hard to understand exactly how wide until the
        data is laid out in front of you. For example, last year, companies with a mixed-gender
        founding
        team saw approximately 11.4 percent of VC capital invested compared to only 2.7 percent
        invested
        in solely female-lead teams.</p>
    <p>The charts below look at 11 years of investment trends for female-founded startups compared
        to
        mixed-gender startups.&nbsp;</p>

        </div>
    </div>
    <p>As you can see from the data above, this tells a greater story than simply pointing out the
        gender gap. What’s not mentioned in many other stories, though, is that funding for
        women-led
        startups is trending upwards. Of course, we still have a long way to go but there are some
        ways
        in which the status quo is already changing — female VCs, for example.&nbsp;</p>
    <h2>Women-led VC funds crushing the gender gap&nbsp;</h2>
    <p>When it comes to venture capital, there’s a financial incentive to close the gender gap:
        greater
        diversity yields higher returns. According to a <a
            href="https://www.bcg.com/en-us/publications/2018/why-women-owned-startups-are-better-bet"
            target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">BCG study</a>, women-founded startups are the
        horse VCs should be betting on. They found that for every dollar of funding, these startups
        generated 78 cents, whereas male-founded startups generated only 31 cents.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>Yet, the data shows that VCs don’t trend towards women, at least not at the rate of
        mixed-gender
        or male-founded startups. Not only is there a gender gap in which startups receive funding,
        but
        there’s also a significant gap in women investors. <a
            href="https://www.axios.com/venture-capital-women-tech-diversity-29c3f2f0-2d1e-4ec5-b542-7878ab149d45.html"
            target="_blank" rel="noopener">Fewer than 10 percent</a> of decision-makers at U.S. VC
        firms
        are women. This means that even though dozens of firms have made concerted efforts to
        diversify
        their ranks, only 105 investors out of roughly 1,088 were female.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>A lack of female-led funds is one of many reasons why the funding gap for women continues to
        be
        wide. However, despite the significant gap, there are a number of female-led venture capital
        funds that are helping bridge the gender gap.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>If you’re a female founder, these 10 funds should be on your radar.</p>
    <div>
        <div>

                <div class="founder-card" tabindex="0">
                    <div class="founder-card-inner">
                        <div class="founder-card-front">
                            <img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E"
                                alt="" data-lazy-src="https://website.embroker.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/11-Tola-Capital.svg">
                        </div>
                        <div class="founder-card-flipped">
                            <img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E"

                </div>

                </div>
            </section>










        </div>
    </div>
    <h2>Advice for female-founders looking to “make it” in the startup world</h2>
    <p>There’s no doubt that data can give startup founders valuable insights, but there’s nothing
        quite
        like tangible advice from those who’ve been there to guide entrepreneurs in the right
        direction.
        To give more women entrepreneurs insights on how they can succeed in the dog-eat-dog world
        of
        venture capital, we turned to female founders and seasoned experts in the startup world to
        gather venture capital insights and advice on how to succeed in an industry that’s largely
        dominated by men.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>Consider the words of wisdom from these nine female leaders.&nbsp;</p>
    <h3>Seek funding from female VCs</h3>
    <p><a href="https://management.buffalo.edu/faculty/academic-departments/marketing/faculty/kim-saxton.html"
            target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
            aria-label="M. Kim Saxton (opens in a new tab)">M.
            Kim Saxton</a>, an angel investor and startup co-founder, is also a marketing strategist and seasoned professor, currently at the University at Buffalo School of Management. Her
        advice spoke about the rise of female VCs and the value of pitching them as a female
        founder.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>“Women tend to solve problems important to women. But men, who tend to be the funders, don’t
        understand these problems or why they are important. One example — Rent the Runway founder
        Jenny
        Hyman tells that she had to frame the problem as being similar to men renting tuxedos before
        she
        could get funding. This has led to the creation of funders who only invest in women-founded
        startups, like Golden Seeds and SoGal Ventures among others. So, one tip is to seek funds
        from
        them.”</p>
    <figure class="wp-block-image"></figure>
    <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-11209 size-full ff-image-desktop"
            src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201435%20522'%3E%3C/svg%3E"
            alt="Kim Saxton Quote" width="1435" height="522" data-lazy-src="https://website.embroker.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/EB-quote-01-M-Kim-Saxton.png?strip=all&lossy=1&ssl=1"></p>

    <h3>Present your product or service from the male perspective.</h3>
    <p>Similar to Saxton’s advice, Stacy Caprio, the founder of <a
            href="http://acceleratedgrowthmarketing.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Growth
            Marketing</a>, offered insights about the male-female divide in venture capital. Because
        female-founded startups often solve problems women have, her advice was to learn to present
        your
        product’s benefits from a male perspective.</p>
    <p>“My advice to female founders who want to raise venture capital is to either make sure you
        present your product’s market and benefits from a male-perspective, or make sure you are
        pitching to a female group of VCs. The audience listening to your pitch is only going to
        want to
        back you if they have a personal connection or can easily see the <a href="https://www.embroker.com/blog/startup-venture-capital-terms/">product-market fit</a> your
        company has. If you are able to turn your pitch so men can connect with it and clearly see
        the
        market, that’s when you’ll start to get more funding. Or simply find women you can pitch to
        if
        your product has no male audience product-market fit connection.”</p>
    <h3>Understand your financials.</h3>
    <p>Bryanne Leeming is the founder and CEO of <a href="https://www.unrulysplats.com/"
            target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
            aria-label="Unruly Studios (opens in a new tab)">Unruly
            Studios</a>, a female-founded edtech company. Her advice speaks to the importance of
        understanding your financials to set your startup apart.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>“My advice for women founders is to build great companies and know your numbers. The numbers
        speak for themselves, especially sales. As you grow, knowing your numbers cold and
        understanding
        the fundamental financial metrics that run your business will set you apart for investors
        and
        allow you to lead your company’s growth, too. If you don’t understand your finances, find a
        mentor who can teach you and dive in.”</p>
    <figure class="wp-block-image"></figure>
    <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-11210 size-full ff-image-desktop"
            src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201435%20420'%3E%3C/svg%3E"
            alt="Bryanne Leeming quote" width="1435" height="420" data-lazy-src="https://website.embroker.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/EB-quote-02-Bryanne-Leeming.png?strip=all&lossy=1&ssl=1"> 
    <h3>Surround yourself with mentors and cohorts who can help your business.</h3>
    <p>Chrissa McFarlane, the CEO and founder of <a href="https://patientory.com/" target="_blank"
            rel="noreferrer noopener" aria-label="Patientory (opens in a new tab)">Patientory</a> is
        no
        stranger to the struggles of the Silicon Valley VC ecosystem. Chrissa made headlines for
        raising
        $7.2 million in three days through online blockchain token sales of her company, Patientory,
        and
        offers her advice:</p>
    <p>“Make it a priority to build an ecosystem of mentors and cohorts who can offer support and
        resources to help your business grow. This ecosystem can provide you with opportunities to
        keep
        you on track such as access to invitations to events that will enable you to connect with
        people, or resources to help expand different aspects of your business, marketing know-how
        to
        help grow the company, financial expertise to help smooth out day-to-day operations, or just
        validation about your business plan with business coaching and support. These are all
        necessary
        and important resources to help your startup succeed.”</p>
    <h3>Don’t let modesty guide you.</h3>
    <p>Michelle Murray is the founder and Managing Director of <a
            href="https://www.seguepartners.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
            aria-label="Segue (opens in a new tab)">Segue</a>,
        a business that provides contract CFO services for startups and venture capital funds (the company was acquired by JTC in 2021).
        Personal
        experience has taught her how important it is to not hold back on talking about your
        accomplishments, especially when it comes to meeting investors.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>“Toot your own horn! Be sure to not let your modesty guide you when it comes to sharing your
        accomplishments. All too often I see men “bragging” about their resume but the women sit
        back
        and don’t want to come across “that way”, so then their accomplishments are overlooked. When
        it
        comes to leading a company and meeting investor milestones what you have done in the past is
        key
        to investors having confidence in your potential for success this time around.”&nbsp;</p>
    <figure class="wp-block-image"></figure>
    <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-11211 size-full ff-image-desktop"
            src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201435%20482'%3E%3C/svg%3E"
            alt="Michelle Murray Quote" width="1435" height="482" data-lazy-src="https://website.embroker.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/EB-quote-03-Michelle-Murray.png?strip=all&lossy=1&ssl=1"> 
    <h3>Know how to negotiate.</h3>
    <p>As a counselor of numerous startups and a business leader at biotech startup <a
            href="https://mannamolecular.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
            aria-label=" (opens in a new tab)">Manna Molecular Science</a>, Rachel Braun Scherl
        comes to
        the table with some valuable advice, specifically around the art of negotiation.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>“Know how to negotiate. This concept covers so many different situations — fundraising,
        partnerships, your salary, someone else’s salary, <a href="https://www.embroker.com/blog/startup-equity-calculator/">equity stakes</a>. The answer is always no if
        you
        don’t ask. So come armed with the facts, the data, the key points whenever you enter a
        negotiation. At least, when a negotiation works out — when both parties have come away with
        something of value, I literally feel a rush of endorphins (the same feeling you get after a
        strenuous workout). In my mind, negotiating is never about decimating the other side, but
        finding solutions that are mutually beneficial, the proverbial ‘win-win.’”&nbsp;</p>
    <h3>Ask for more money than you think you’ll need.</h3>
    <p>Julie Weldon and Stacey Pierce are entrepreneurs, <a href="https://www.podomatic.com/podcasts/womenentrepreneursgrowglobal/episodes/2025-01-14T08_12_41-08_00"
            target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
            aria-label=" (opens in a new tab)">podcasters</a>,
        and co-founders of <a href="https://omegear.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
            aria-label=" (opens in a new tab)">O.M.E. Gear</a>, an outdoor gear company based in
        Charleston, South Carolina. These two are well-versed in the trials and tribulations that
        come
        with being not only women in the startup world, but also as an LGBT couple. Their words of
        wisdom speak to finances and using working capital to build your business.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
    <p>“Another piece of advice we would give is to always ask for more than you think you are going
        to
        need. Do this by splitting up your ask into tranches. Do not count on sales to launch your
        business into the profitable zone immediately out of the gate. You will need the extra money
        to
        fund your efforts while building your business. Don’t worry; investors realize this and any
        savvy investor will understand you need working capital so you can focus on what you need to
        be
        successful.”</p>
    <figure class="wp-block-image"></figure>
    <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-11212 size-full ff-image-desktop"
            src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201435%20417'%3E%3C/svg%3E"
            alt="quote by Julie Weldon &amp; Stacey Pierce" width="1435" height="417" data-lazy-src="https://website.embroker.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/EB-quote-04-Julie-Weldon-Stacey-Pierce.png?strip=all&lossy=1&ssl=1">
    <h3>Network within your industry.</h3>
    <p>The basic litmus test that VC funds run on founders is if they can get an introduction to the
        firm via networking. These days, <a href="https://www.embroker.com/blog/series-a-venture-capital/">VCs expect founders to use their networks</a> and get an
        introduction. Networking shows three important things: (1) a founder’s understanding of how
        VC
        works, (2) the ability to hustle to get the intro, and (3) a founder can build a trusted
        connection via someone who already knows them.</p>
    <p>Jessica David, the Director of Marketing at <a href="https://www.seventysixcapital.com/"
            target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" aria-label=" (opens in a new tab)">SeventySix
            Capital</a> and Forbes 30 Under 30 honoree know a thing or two about networking and
        building
        relationships with other leaders in your industry. After all, networking can be a crucial
        component of raising venture capital.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>“My best advice for female founders is to participate in the ecosystem within your industry
        as
        much as possible. It’s not just a matter of showing up; engage with others, follow up, and
        remain persistent. Speak with clarity and confidence! Use each meeting or event as an
        opportunity to <a href="https://www.embroker.com/blog/series-a-pitch-deck/">strengthen your pitch</a>.”</p>
    <h3>Attract like-minded people by being yourself.</h3>
    <p>Our last piece of advice comes from Dr. Radhika Dirks, the CEO of <a href="https://xlabs-ai.com/"
            target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
            aria-label="XLabs (opens in a new tab)">XLabs</a>
        — an innovation agency that reimagines the future via AI, unconventional computing and
        neurotech. She reminds women that being your true self is a surefire way to attract the
        right
        people to your startup, especially investors.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>“Do and be YOU fully. If that includes being feminine, be that. Female leaders do not need to
        simulate or mimic men or worse, hide issues specific to them, to lead anymore — this still
        comes
        as a surprise to most of us. When we are ourselves, we attract people — men and women — to
        bolster each other. I remember the first team dinner at XLabs where we hosted a group of
        future
        employees. We had about 13 people around the table and we not only had 70% PhDs around the
        table
        — in different fields — but we had more women PhDs than men, without even trying to
        explicitly
        attract more women on the team. The tides are changing, slowly, but changing, so do not
        compromise who you are at any time.”</p>
    <h2>The value of investing in female founders</h2>
    <p>Despite the data that trends upward, breaking new ground in terms of closing the gender gap
        between female and male founders on the quest for funding is an uphill climb. Venture
        capitalists, angel investors, and others writing the checks hold the greatest power to fuel
        change, and the research shows they should.&nbsp;</p>
    <h3>Female founders outperform males.</h3>
    <p>Earlier we discussed a recent study from BCG that found for every dollar of investment
        raised,
        female-run startups generated 78 cents in revenue, whereas male-run startups generated a
        fraction of that.</p>
    <p>This data is also consistent with other studies: take the data collected by <a
            href="http://10years.firstround.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
            aria-label=" (opens in a new tab)">First Round Capital</a>, for example. They found that
        the female-founded companies it had funded performed 63% better than the all-male
        founding
        teams it had funded. <a
            href="https://www.kauffmanfellows.org/journal/the-rising-tide-a-learning-by-investing-initiative-to-bridge-the-gender-gap"
            target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" aria-label=" (opens in a new tab)">The
            Kauffman
            Fellows Report</a> also found that women-led teams generate a 35% higher return on
        investment than all-male teams.</p>
    <h3>Women are more likely to prioritize corporate social responsibility.</h3>
    <p>Now more than ever, how a business conducts itself, ethically speaking, can change the
        trajectory
        of success. So, in today’s ecosystem where the vast majority of consumers are willing to buy
        a
        product or service based on a company’s social and internal values, <a
            href="https://www.embroker.com/blog/business-ethics-and-social-responsibility/"
            target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" aria-label=" (opens in a new tab)">corporate
            social responsibility</a> matters.&nbsp;</p>
    <p><a href="https://newsroom.haas.berkeley.edu/more-female-board-directors-add-improved-sustainability-performance/"
            target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
            aria-label=" (opens in a new tab)">Research</a>
        shows that female-led companies are more likely to prioritize socially responsible
        initiatives.
        For example, research by Kellie McElhaney, the founder of the Center for Gender Equity &amp;
        Leadership at the University of California at Berkeley’s Haas School of Business, found that
        the
        number of women on a corporate board directly correlates with a firm’s sustainability
        performance.</p>
    <h3>Female founders are less motivated by money.</h3>
    <p>Contrary to popular belief, entrepreneurship is not a get rich quick scheme, especially in
        the
        startup game. Sure, <a href="https://www.embroker.com/blog/unicorn-startups/" target="_blank"
            rel="noreferrer noopener" aria-label=" (opens in a new tab)">unicorns exist</a>, but the
        most successful entrepreneurs see money as a byproduct of entrepreneurship.&nbsp;</p>
    <p>Because of the wide gender gap that exists in the startup world, women-founders are
        constantly
        having to prove their personal and business worth. As a result, female founders are more
        intrinsically motivated than men and more likely to go the extra mile when faced with
        business
        challenges. When push comes to shove, they’ll make the sacrifices necessary to maximize the
        longevity and long-term prospects of the business.</p>
    <p>By investing in female founders, not only will you be able to fuel your level of impact, but
        it’s likely that you’ll get more bang for your buck.&nbsp;</p>

							<em class="font-heading-4 tw-font-semibold tw-not-italic">Startup Insurance Calculator</em>

        ecosystem. <a href="https://www.embroker.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"

<script>window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
function flipStart() {
    jQuery('.founder-card').mouseenter(function() {
        jQuery(this).find('.founder-card-inner').addClass('active');
        
    }).mouseleave(function() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            jQuery(this).find('.founder-card-inner').removeClass('active');
        }.bind(this), 1000);
    })

    jQuery('.founder-card').focus(function() {
        jQuery(this).find('.founder-card-inner').addClass('active');
        
    }).blur(function() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            jQuery(this).find('.founder-card-inner').removeClass('active');
        }.bind(this), 1000);
    })
    
}
    


function flipDelay() {
    jQuery(this).removeClass('active');
}


jQuery(flipStart);

function toggleMapInfo() {
   
    let domRank = document.getElementById('map-rank');
    let domName = document.getElementById('map-name');
    let domCapital = document.getElementById('map-capital');
    let domDeals = document.getElementById('map-deals');

    // Display #1 Most Expensive City on Page Load
    jQuery('#sanfrancisco').children( '.cls-6' ).css("fill", "#ff7847");

    jQuery(domRank).html(jQuery('#sanfrancisco').data("rank"));
    jQuery(domName).html(jQuery('#sanfrancisco').data("name"));
    jQuery(domCapital).html(jQuery('#sanfrancisco').data("capital"));
    jQuery(domDeals).html(jQuery('#sanfrancisco').data("deals"));

    // Hide #1 Most Expensive City on Page Load (Desktop)
    if ( jQuery(window).width() > 1025 ) {
        jQuery('#sanfrancisco').children( '.cls-5' ).css("fill", "#6673ff");
        jQuery('#map-info-container').css("display", "none");
    }
    

    // Show info on click
    jQuery('#interactive-map > g').hover(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-normal' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-toggled' ).css("display", "block");
        // Reset Washington pin to normal
        jQuery('#sanfrancisco').children( '.cls-5' ).css("fill", "#6673ff"); 
        jQuery('#map-info-container').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let rank = jQuery(this).data("rank");
        let name = jQuery(this).data("name");
        let capital = jQuery(this).data("capital");
        let deals = jQuery(this).data("deals");

        jQuery(domRank).html(rank);
        jQuery(domName).html(name);
        jQuery(domCapital).html(capital);
        jQuery(domDeals).html(deals);

        let $window = jQuery(window);
        let $infoContainer = jQuery('#map-info-container');

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 1025 ) {
            let offset = jQuery(this).offset();
            let pointerX = offset.left;
            let pointerY = offset.top - 25;

            $infoContainer.css({
                top: pointerY - $infoContainer.height() - 30,
                left: Math.min(pointerX - (($infoContainer.width() / 2) - 20), $window.width() - $infoContainer.width()),
            });
        } else {
            $infoContainer.css({
                top: 'auto',
                left: 'auto',
            });
        }
    });

    jQuery('#interactive-map > g').click(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-normal' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-toggled' ).css("display", "block");
        // Reset Washington pin to normal
        jQuery('#sanfrancisco').children( '.cls-5' ).css("fill", "#6673ff"); 
        jQuery('#map-info-container').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let rank = jQuery(this).data("rank");
        let name = jQuery(this).data("name");
        let capital = jQuery(this).data("capital");
        let deals = jQuery(this).data("deals");

        jQuery(domRank).html(rank);
        jQuery(domName).html(name);
        jQuery(domCapital).html(capital);
        jQuery(domDeals).html(deals);

        let $window = jQuery(window);
        let $infoContainer = jQuery('#map-info-container');

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 1025 ) {
            let offset = jQuery(this).offset();
            let pointerX = offset.left;
            let pointerY = offset.top - 25;

            $infoContainer.css({
                top: pointerY - $infoContainer.height() - 30,
                left: Math.min(pointerX - (($infoContainer.width() / 2) - 20), $window.width() - $infoContainer.width()),
            });
        } else {
            $infoContainer.css({
                top: 'auto',
                left: 'auto',
            });
        }
    });

    // Show info on focus for keyboard users
    jQuery('#interactive-map > g').focusin(function() {       
        jQuery('#map-info-container').css("display", "block");


        // Toggle bigger pin for clicked city
        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-normal' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-toggled' ).css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let rank = jQuery(this).data("rank");
        let name = jQuery(this).data("name");
        let capital = jQuery(this).data("capital");
        let deals = jQuery(this).data("deals");


        jQuery(domRank).html(rank);
        jQuery(domName).html(name);
        jQuery(domCapital).html(capital);
        jQuery(domDeals).html(deals);

    })

    // Reset pins on mouseleave
    jQuery('#interactive-map > g').mouseleave(function(){
        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-normal' ).css("display", "block");
        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-toggled' ).css("display", "none");

        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 1025 ) {
            jQuery('#map-info-container').css("display", "none");
        }
        
    })

    // Reset pins when unfocused
    jQuery('#interactive-map > g').focusout(function(){
        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-normal' ).css("display", "block");
        jQuery(this).children( '.pin-toggled' ).css("display", "none");
    })
}


jQuery(toggleMapInfo);

function toggleGraph() {

    let domFemaleYear = document.getElementById('female-year');
    let domMixedYear = document.getElementById('mixed-gender-year');
    let domFemaleDealCount = document.getElementById('female-deal-count');
    let domMixedDealCount = document.getElementById('mixed-gender-deal-count');
    let domFemaleVCYear = document.getElementById('female-year-vc');
    let domFemaleVC = document.getElementById('female-vc');
    let domMixedVC = document.getElementById('mixed-gender-vc');
    let domMixedVCYear = document.getElementById('mixed-gender-year-vc');


    jQuery('#deal-count-chart > .female-dc-data').hover(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "block");

        jQuery('.graph-info-box-female').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let femaleYear = jQuery(this).data("female-year");
        let femaleDealCount = jQuery(this).data("female-dealcount");


        jQuery(domFemaleYear).html(femaleYear);
        jQuery(domFemaleDealCount).html(femaleDealCount);

        // jQuery(domCapital).html(capital);
        // jQuery(domDeals).html(deals);

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 700 ) {

            var offset = jQuery('.female-dc-data').offset();
            var relativeX = (e.pageX - offset.left);
            var relativeY = (e.pageY - offset.top);
            let pointerX = relativeX - 50;
            let pointerY = relativeY + 300;
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-female').css({'top':pointerY,'left':pointerX}); 
        }
    });

    jQuery('#deal-count-chart > .mixed-dc-data').hover(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "block");

        jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let mixedYear = jQuery(this).data("year");
        let mixedDealCount = jQuery(this).data("mixed-dealcount");


    
        jQuery(domMixedYear).html(mixedYear);
        jQuery(domMixedDealCount).html(mixedDealCount);
        // jQuery(domCapital).html(capital);
        // jQuery(domDeals).html(deals);

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 700 ) {

            var offset = jQuery('.mixed-dc-data').offset();
            var relativeX = (e.pageX - offset.left);
            var relativeY = (e.pageY - offset.top);
            let pointerX = relativeX - 50;
            let pointerY = relativeY + 260;
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender').css({'top':pointerY,'left':pointerX}); 
        }
    });

    jQuery('#vc-chart > .female-vc-data').hover(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "block");

        jQuery('.graph-info-box-female-vc').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let FemaleVCYear = jQuery(this).data("year");
        let femaleVC = jQuery(this).data("vc");


        jQuery(domFemaleVCYear).html(FemaleVCYear);
        jQuery(domFemaleVC).html(femaleVC);

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 700 ) {

            var offset = jQuery('.female-vc-data').offset();
            var relativeX = (e.pageX - offset.left);
            var relativeY = (e.pageY - offset.top);
            let pointerX = relativeX - 50;
            let pointerY = relativeY + 300;
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-female-vc').css({'top':pointerY,'left':pointerX}); 
        }
    });

    jQuery('#vc-chart > .mixed-vc-data').hover(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "block");

        jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender-vc').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let mixedVCYear = jQuery(this).data("year");
        let mixedVC = jQuery(this).data("vc");


        jQuery(domMixedVCYear).html(mixedVCYear);
        jQuery(domMixedVC).html(mixedVC);

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 700 ) {

            var offset = jQuery('.mixed-vc-data').offset();
            var relativeX = (e.pageX - offset.left);
            var relativeY = (e.pageY - offset.top);
            let pointerX = relativeX - 50;
            let pointerY = relativeY + 260;
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender-vc').css({'top':pointerY,'left':pointerX}); 
        }
    });


    jQuery('#deal-count-chart > .female-dc-data, #deal-count-chart > .mixed-dc-data, #vc-chart > .mixed-vc-data, #vc-chart > .female-vc-data').mouseleave(function(){
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "block");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "none");

        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 1025 ) {
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-female, .graph-info-box-mixed-gender, .graph-info-box-female-vc, .graph-info-box-mixed-gender-vc').css("display", "none");
        }
        
    })

    // FOCUS --------------------------------------------------------------
    jQuery('#vc-chart > .mixed-vc-data').focusin(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "block");

        jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender-vc').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let mixedVCYear = jQuery(this).data("year");
        let mixedVC = jQuery(this).data("vc");


        jQuery(domMixedVCYear).html(mixedVCYear);
        jQuery(domMixedVC).html(mixedVC);

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender-vc').css('top', '45%');
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender-vc').css('left', '30%');

            if ( jQuery(window).width() > 601 ) {
                jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender-vc').css('top', '35%');
            }
       
    });

    jQuery('#deal-count-chart > .female-dc-data').focusin(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "block");

        jQuery('.graph-info-box-female').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let femaleYear = jQuery(this).data("female-year");
        let femaleDealCount = jQuery(this).data("female-dealcount");


        jQuery(domFemaleYear).html(femaleYear);
        jQuery(domFemaleDealCount).html(femaleDealCount);

        // jQuery(domCapital).html(capital);
        // jQuery(domDeals).html(deals);

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-female').css('top', '45%');
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-female').css('left', '30%');  

            if ( jQuery(window).width() > 601 ) {
                jQuery('.graph-info-box-female').css('top', '35%');
            }

    });

    jQuery('#deal-count-chart > .mixed-dc-data').focusin(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "block");

        jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let mixedYear = jQuery(this).data("year");
        let mixedDealCount = jQuery(this).data("mixed-dealcount");


    
        jQuery(domMixedYear).html(mixedYear);
        jQuery(domMixedDealCount).html(mixedDealCount);
        // jQuery(domCapital).html(capital);
        // jQuery(domDeals).html(deals);

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender').css('top', '45%');
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender').css('left', '30%');

            if ( jQuery(window).width() > 601 ) {
                jQuery('.graph-info-box-mixed-gender').css('top', '35%');
            }
        
    });


    jQuery('#vc-chart > .female-vc-data').focusin(function(e){

        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "none");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "block");

        jQuery('.graph-info-box-female-vc').css("display", "block");

        // Add data to the info box
        let FemaleVCYear = jQuery(this).data("year");
        let femaleVC = jQuery(this).data("vc");


        jQuery(domFemaleVCYear).html(FemaleVCYear);
        jQuery(domFemaleVC).html(femaleVC);

        // Move the info box to the clicked pin on desktop
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-female-vc').css('top', '45%');
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-female-vc').css('left', '30%');

            if ( jQuery(window).width() > 601 ) {
                jQuery('.graph-info-box-female-vc').css('top', '35%');
            }
        
    });

    jQuery('#deal-count-chart > .female-dc-data, #deal-count-chart > .mixed-dc-data, #vc-chart > .mixed-vc-data, #vc-chart > .female-vc-data').focusout(function(){
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-little' ).css("display", "block");
        jQuery(this).children( '.bullet-big' ).css("display", "none");

        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 1025 ) {
            jQuery('.graph-info-box-female, .graph-info-box-mixed-gender, .graph-info-box-female-vc, .graph-info-box-mixed-gender-vc').css("display", "none");
        }
        
    })

    
}

jQuery(toggleGraph);

chartInt = 1;
chartNext = 2;

jQuery(document).ready(function() {
    jQuery("#piecharts > .pie-chart-single#1").fadeIn(700);
    toolTip();
});


function prev() {
    newChart = chartInt -1;
    showChart(newChart);
    if (newChart <= 1) {
        newChart = 18;
        showChart(newChart);
    }
}

function next() {
    newChart = chartInt +1;
    showChart(newChart);
    if (newChart > 18) {
        newChart = 1;
        showChart(newChart);
    }
}

// BUTTON FOCUS --------------------------------------------------------

jQuery('#leftarrow').keydown(function(e) {
    let keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
    if(keycode == '13'){
        newChart = chartInt -1;
        showChart(newChart);
    }
})

jQuery('#rightarrow').keydown(function(e) {
    let keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
    if(keycode == '13'){
        newChart = chartInt -1;
        showChart(newChart);
    } else {
        jQuery('#rightarrow').css("outline", "0 !important");
    }
})

function showChart(id) {
    count = jQuery('#piecharts > .pie-chart-single').id;
    if (id > count) {
        id = 1;
    } else if (id < 1) {
        id = count;
    }

    jQuery('#piecharts > .pie-chart-single#' + chartInt).fadeOut(400);
    jQuery('#piecharts > .pie-chart-single#'+ id).fadeIn(400);

    chartInt = id;
    chartNext = id +1;
}

function toolTip() {

    jQuery('.pie-chart-single svg .cls-13, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-12, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-14').hover(function(e){

        jQuery('.tool-tip-container').css("display", "block");
    
        // Add data to the info box
        jQuery('#tool-tip-title').html(jQuery(this).data('title'));
        jQuery('#tool-tip-deal').html(jQuery(this).data('deal'));
        jQuery('#tool-tip-capital').html(jQuery(this).data('capital'));

        // Set the bottom border of the tool tip title to the color associated with the category
        if (jQuery(this).data('title') === "Late VC") {
            jQuery('#tool-tip-title').css('border-bottom', '3px solid #21E6AD');
        } 
        else if (jQuery(this).data('title') === "Early VC") {
            jQuery('#tool-tip-title').css('border-bottom', '3px solid #1AB8E8');
        } else {
            jQuery('#tool-tip-title').css('border-bottom', '3px solid #B45EF9');
        }

    
        // Move the info box to the hovered section on desktop
        if ( jQuery(window).width() > 700 ) {
    
            var tooltipOffset = jQuery(this).offset();
            var containerOffset = jQuery('.pie-chart-container').offset();
            let pointerX = (tooltipOffset.left - containerOffset.left) + 125;
            let pointerY = (tooltipOffset.top - containerOffset.top) + 90;
            
            jQuery('.tool-tip-container').css({top: pointerY, left: pointerX}); 
        }
    
        // Hide tool tip when the mouse leaves the section
        jQuery('.pie-chart-single svg .cls-13, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-12, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-14').mouseleave(function() {
            jQuery('.tool-tip-container').css('display', 'none');
        })
    });


    // FOCUS ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    jQuery('.pie-chart-single svg .cls-13, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-12, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-14').keypress(function(e){
        if((e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which) == 13){

        jQuery('.tool-tip-container').css("display", "block");
    
        // Add data to the info box
        jQuery('#tool-tip-title').html(jQuery(this).data('title'));
        jQuery('#tool-tip-deal').html(jQuery(this).data('deal'));
        jQuery('#tool-tip-capital').html(jQuery(this).data('capital'));
    
        // Set the bottom border of the tool tip title to the color associated with the category
        if (jQuery(this).data('title') === "Late VC") {
            jQuery('#tool-tip-title').css('border-bottom', '3px solid #ff6138');
        } 
        else if (jQuery(this).data('title') === "Early VC") {
            jQuery('#tool-tip-title').css('border-bottom', '3px solid #74bcf1');
        } else {
            jQuery('#tool-tip-title').css('border-bottom', '3px solid #798bff');
        }

    
    
        // Move the info box to the hovered section on desktop
        // if ( jQuery(window).width() > 700 ) {
    
        //     var offset = jQuery('.pie-charts').offset();
        //     var relativeX = (e.pageX - offset.left);
        //     var relativeY = (e.pageY - offset.top);
        //     let pointerX = relativeX + 50;
        //     let pointerY = relativeY - 90;
        //     jQuery('.tool-tip-container').css({'top':pointerY,'left':pointerX}); 
        // }
    
        // Hide tool tip when the mouse leaves the section
        jQuery('.pie-chart-single svg .cls-13, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-12, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-14').mouseleave(function() {
            jQuery('.tool-tip-container').css('display', 'none');
        })

        jQuery('.pie-chart-single svg .cls-13, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-12, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-14').css("outline", "1 !important");
    } else {
        jQuery('.pie-chart-single svg .cls-13, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-12, .pie-chart-single svg .cls-14').css("outline", "0 !important");
    }
    });



}
